 yoga aapako kisi dal ke adheen nahin karata he

 yoga kii utpatti dharm kii aadhunik samaj par chhapi kitabon ke kisi bhi panne se nahin hoti he
 'yogis were able to increase their health and age by learning yogas like postures, postures, pranayam etc
 from snakes, frogs, etc

 1935 main gitapress yoga ke vishwaroop par ank nikaal saktaa he to aaj ham kyon or kisase bhaybheet hai
 Yoga does not make a coward
 yoga aapako kisi dal ke adheen nahin karata he
 No religious political ideology should be propagated in the name of yoga
 yoga kii utpatti dharm kii aadhunik samaj par chhapi kitabon ke kisi bhi panne se nahin hoti he
 'yogis were able to increase their health and age by learning yogas like postures, postures, pranayam etc
 from snakes, frogs, etc

 ' aaj yoga ko bhartiyata kii pahchaan bataate hue hindutv se jodne kaa prayaas ho rahaa he

 jabaki yoga kaa kabhi daawa nahin rahaa ki wo kisi kii satta ko banaae yaa bachaae rakhane ke liye saadhan banegaa

 There could have been a meaningful philosophical debate about yoga, but it has been converted into a package of rugs

 Is Yoga being separated from all traditions? 'kalyaan' ke is ank main ek lekh he- isai-dharm yoga kaa sthaan
 Reverend Edwin Grebz wrote
 isai dharm main bhi paramatma se ekaakaar ho jane par jor diya gaya he
 Grebz writes that at the time of starting the sermon, there is a description that Jesus Christ had fasted for forty days, but he did not seem to have done this penance as a means, but for some time he stayed in the forest alone and there He was so engrossed in thinking about his future teaching work that he was unable to eat or drink
 isai dharm main yoga ke hone kii dharna par lambii bahes he
 Our Mahatmas have also discussed it a lot, but is there a slight symptom of this generosity in the current era
 isi ank main kabir yoga kaa zikr he
 The same Kabir who has expressed his disbelief at the name of separation between Hindus and Muslims
 buddha, jain yoga par bhi vistaar se ek lekh he
 The basic meaning of all yoga and its ultimate culmination is in union with God
 to kya is lihaaz se sufi yogi nahin hue
 Namazi did not become a yogi or did not do yoga in Islam
 yoga kii vidhi kya sirf asana he
 i think yoga cannot be more compressed than this
 'kalyaan' ke yogank main shri ech jahangir toraporewala kaa lekh he jo zarathosti dharm main yoga kii talash karte hai
 In Parsi religion too, the paths of knowledge, devotion and karma have been mentioned, even though the word yoga has not been used in our remaining texts
 aisa koun sa darshan he jiskaa ek rup parivartit hokar duusare dharm main nahin dikhataa
 Who were those people who saw the essence of all religions in the attainment of one God and were told that God is one
 ye log koun hai jo sabhi dharmon ke ishwar ko alag-alag bataane main lage hue hai
 i also do not mean that Yoga is not Indian, Yoga cannot be imagined without Indian philosophy and principles, but why are we not talking about the diversity of Yoga
 yoga aapako dharmik nahin banaata he
 Rather, it frees us from rituals and gives us the power to see God within ourselves
 us shakti ko aap tivi dekhakar yaa kisi yogi kii banaai sidi dekhakar hasil nahin kar sakate hai
 Why is there no question of sadhana and samadhi
 yoga kaa arth chetana ke jaagrit staron ko bhi hasil karnaa he
 Maharishi Arvind has written that no man should ever set foot on this path, who is not sure that this is the call of our conscience and we are ready to walk on this path till the end
 tippaniyan 'I mean this little ego is a creation of nature as well as a mental, natural and physical creation
 jab sadatma mil jaataa he tab ahankaar kaa kaam puraa ho jaataa he phir uski koi upyogita nahin rah jaati he

 us saal mahaj 12 fisadi chaatr hi dasvin kii pariksha main safal ho paae the
 He said that the level of education in Bihar is so bad that whenever the government stops cheating, the number of students passing that year decreases incredibly
 saalon se bihar main parikshaon main bade paimaane par nakal karwaane kaa prachlan rahaa he
 This includes the parents of the examinees from their relatives
 har saal march main media se lekar soshal media tak main nakal kii khabaren or tasviren chaa jaati hai
 But this year, the Education Department has taken several steps to prevent cheating in the examinations of tenth and twelfth in February and March respectively
 shiksha vibhaag ne adhikariyon ko nirdesh diya he ki ve pariksha kendron par sisitivi camera lagavaayen or unka sidhaa prasaaran internet par karaane kii vyavastha karen
 Apart from this, additional security forces should also be deployed
 shiksha mantri ashok choudhary ne bataaya, "ham parikshaon main nakal ko or bardaasht nahin karenge

 " choudhary ne kaha ki agar koi nakal kii koshish karata he to uske khilaaf kade kadam uthaae jaaenge
 According to education department officials, 14 lakh candidates will be included in the twelfth examination to be held in the last week of February and 15 lakh candidates will appear in the tenth examination in March
 bihar skool pariksha samiti ke chairman lalakeshwar prasad singh ne bataaya ki pariksha centre ke baahar sisitivi camera lage honge or pariksha kendron ke andar kii videography karai jaaegi or pariksha kendron par hajaaron surakshakarmiyon kii tainaati kii jaaegi
 He informed that all the District Magistrates and Superintendents of Police have been asked to apply Section 144 around the examination centers one hour before the commencement of the examination and do not allow people to gather illegally
 khaastaur se parikshaarthi ke abhibhavakon, rishtedaaron or mitron ko pariksha centre se dur rakhaa jaae
 State Chief Secretary Anjani Kumar Singh chaired a high-level meeting on Tuesday in which it was decided to cancel the examination and take action against the concerned officers and teachers if any copying information is received at any center
 araval jile ke ek sarkari skool ke shikshak gajendra sharma kaa kahana he ki pariksha main nakal rokane ke liye yah jaruri kadam he

 After bowling Virender Sehwag on Sunday on the second day of the ongoing second Test match between the Indian cricket team and Australia, the Australian bowler was longing for success throughout the day
 yah najaara bilkul vaisaa hi tha, jaisaa varsh 2001 main border-gavaskar trophy ke duusare test match main bharat kii duusari pari ke dauraan dekhne ko mila tha
 At that time, the experienced Indian batsmen Rahul Dravid and VVS Laxman had brought the Indian team from the brink of defeat due to their excellent batting
 donon ke bich 376 ranon kii mahatvapurn saajhedaari hui thi
 Laxman and Dravid came out to bat for the third three of the match and returned unbeaten on the fourth day
 kangaroo gendbaaj chauthe din wicket ke liye prayaas karte rahe, lekin lakshmana or dravid diwaar banakar unki har niti kaa munhtod jawaab dete rahe
 Dravid had a crucial innings of 180 and Laxman 281 in this match, which helped India win by 171 runs
 uppal sthit rajeev gandhi antarrashtriya cricket stadium main jari test match ke duusare din murali vijay or cheteshwar pujaara ne jis tarah kaa khel dikhaaya usase lakshmana or dravid kii yaaden ek baar phir se taaja ho gayi
 Both young batsmen played in the style of seasoned Test batsmen despite not having much experience of international cricket
 donon ne sahvaag ke out hone ke baad kangaaroon ke dabaav banane ke mansoobon par pani pher diya
 While Murali scored his second Test century, Pujara strengthened his claim of being a Test batsman by scoring a fourth international Test century

 "the film is based on the life of Dasaratha Manjhi, a poor laborer from Gahlor village in Gaya district
 unhen ‘mauten main’ ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa tha
 In memory of his wife, he had made his way from the middle of the mountain using only hammer and chisel
 unki patni ilaaj ke abhaav main mar gai thim kyonki nikatatam aspataal tak pahunchane main is pahaad ke chalate kaaphi samay lagata tha

 navazuddin siddiqui dasharath maanjhi ke kirdaar main hai

 film 21 agast ko relies hogi

 ’’ yah film gaya jile ke gahalor gaanv ke garib majdoor dasharath maanjhi ke jivan par aadhaarit he
 He was also known as 'mountaine Man'
 unhone apni patni kii yaad main bas hathode or chheni ke upyog se hi pahaad ke bich se rasta bana diya tha

 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh hoped that all political ideologies in the Maldives would unite to find a way forward, while Maldives President Mohammad Waheed expressed his deep commitment to elections and democracy
 aadhikarik sutron ne bataaya ki farvari main badalte raajnneetik halaat main satta par kabiz hone ke baad se pehali videsh yatra par nikle wahid ne singh ke saath vyapak vichaar-vimarsh kiya
 During this, he informed the Prime Minister on the current political situation of his country
 raashtrapati wahid ne maldive sarkaar dwaara gathit rashtriya jaanch ayog (ensiai) se jude muddon par bhi singh ko jaankaree di jiskaa gathan saat farvari, 2012 ke ghatnakram kii jaanch ke liye kiya gaya tha, jis din wahid ne mohammad nashid ke istife ke baad pad sambhala
 During the meeting, Singh assured Waheed that India would continue to help Maldives for its development
 sutron ke anusaar unhone kaha ki maldive main shanti or sthirataa bharat ke liye ahm he
 Reiterating his commitment to long-term friendship with India, Waheed insisted on following all the consents
 sutron ne bataaya ki unhone bharat ke samarthan ke liye uskaa aabhaar bhi adaa kiya
 Waheed said that Maldives has looked at India's experiences and example in learning democratic governance
 tippaniyan He can also meet entrepreneurs in his five-day tour and propose Indian investments in the Maldives
 isse pehle, videsh mantri esaem krishna se bhi mulaakaat kar wahid ne dwipaksheeya rishton ke anek pahaluon par charchaa kii
 Official sources said Waheed, who embarked on his first foreign trip since assuming power in the changing political situation in February, held extensive discussions with Singh
 is dauraan unhone apane desh ke maujuuda raajnneetik halaat par pradhanmantri ko jaankaree di
 President Waheed also briefed Singh on issues related to the National Commission of Inquiry (NCI) set up by the Maldives government, which was set up to investigate the developments on February 7, 2012, the day Waheed took office following Mohammad Nasheed's resignation
 
 singh ne mulaakaat ke dauraan wahid ko aashwaasan diya ki maldive ke vikaas ke liye bharat madad karata rahegaa
